renderer.makeVertexTemplatesFromJsonModel(fromVertices, toVertices, uv)[source]¶

This is similar to makeVertexTemplates but is a more convenient when reading off of the json model files. :param fromVertices: from :param toVertices: to :param uv: keywords uv map :return: template for a cube

renderer.makeVerticesFromModel(templates, dataMask=0)[source]¶

Returns a function that creates vertex arrays.

This produces vertex arrays based on the passed templates. This doesn’t cull any faces based on if they are exposed.

Parameters:
  • templates – list of templates to draw
  • dataMask – mask to mask the data
renderer.rendermain()[source]¶
renderer.rotateTemplate(template, x=0, y=0)[source]¶

Rotate template around x-axis and then around y-axis. Both angles must to multiples of 90.
